document.getElementById('toast'); // Build background grid const bgGrid = document.getElementById('bgGrid'); BACKGROUNDS.forEach((bg, i) => { const div = document.createElement('div'); div.className = 'bg-thumb'; div.innerHTML = `
✓
${bg.emoji} ${bg.name}
`; const pc = document.createElement('canvas'); pc.width = 120; pc.height = 90; div.insertBefore(pc, div.firstChild); // Draw thumbnail if (bg._img !== undefined && bg._img === null) { // Image-based bg: load image first then draw real thumbnail const ctx2 = pc.getContext('2d'); // Show simple placeholder while loading ctx2.fillStyle = '#2d1a0e'; ctx2.fillRect(0, 0, 120, 90); ctx2.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,220,120,0.5)'; ctx2.font = '18px serif'; ctx2.textAlign = 'center'; ctx2.textBaseline = 'middle'; ctx2.fillText('⏳', 60, 45); // Load the actual image const thumbImg = new Image(); thumbImg.onload = () => { ctx2.clearRect(0, 0, 120, 90); ctx2.drawImage(thumbImg, 0, 0, 120, 90); bg._img = thumbImg; // cache for use in draw() }; // Get src from the draw function's closure string const fnStr = bg.draw.toString(); const m = fnStr.match(/img\.src\s*=\s*'(data:[^']+)'/); if (m) thumbImg.src = m[1]; } else { bg.draw(pc.getContext('2d'), 120, 90); } div.addEventListener('click', () => { document.querySelectorAll('.bg-thumb').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('selected')); div.classList.add('selected'); selectedBg = bg; document.getElementById('goToCamera').disabled = false; }); bgGrid.appendChild(div); }); // ============================================================ // NAVIGATION // ============================================================ function showScreen(n) { ['screen1','screen2','screen3'].forEach((id,i) => { document.getElementById(id).classList.toggle('active', i+1===n); }); [dot1,dot2,dot3].forEach((d,i) => { d.classList.remove('active','done'); if(i+1 < n) d.classList.add('done'); else if(i+1 === n) d.classList.add('active'); }); } document.getElementById('goToCamera').addEventListener('click', async () => { showScreen(2); await initCamera(); }); document.getElementById('flipBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => { if(!cameraReady) return; facingMode = facingMode === 'user' ? 'environment' : 'user'; // Update flip button tooltip const flipBtn = document.getElementById('flipBtn'); flipBtn.title = facingMode === 'user' ? '切換到後鏡頭' : '切換到前鏡頭'; stopAll(); await initCamera(); }); document.getElementById('backBtn').addEventListener('click', () => { stopAll(); showScreen(1); }); document.getElementById('retakeBtn').addEventListener('click', () => { showScreen(2); initCamera(); }); // ============================================================ // MEDIAPIPE SEGMENTATION // ============================================================ async function initSegmentation() { return new Promise((resolve) => { selfieSegmentation = new SelfieSegmentation({ locateFile: (file) => `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@mediapipe/selfie_segmentation/${file}` }); // model 1 = selfie (close up), model 0 = general (better for rear/full body) const modelSel = facingMode === 'user' ? 1 : 0; selfieSegmentation.setOptions({ modelSelection: modelSel, selfieMode: facingMode === 'user' }); selfieSegmentation.onResults(onSegmentationResults); selfieSegmentation.initialize().then(() => { segmentationReady = true; resolve(); }).catch(err => { console.error('Segmentation init failed:', err); // Fallback: just use video without segmentation segmentationReady = false; resolve(); }); }); } let lastSegResult = null; function onSegmentationResults(results) { lastSegResult = results; } // ============================================================ // CAMERA // ============================================================ async function initCamera() { cameraReady = false; shootBtn.disabled = true; camPrompt.style.display = 'flex'; camPrompt.innerHTML = `
🤖
正在載入 AI 去背模型…
`; try { stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: { facingMode: facingMode, width: { ideal: 640 }, height: { ideal: 854 } }, audio: false }); videoEl.srcObject = stream; await new Promise(r => { videoEl.onloadedmetadata = () => { videoEl.play(); r(); }; }); // Resize canvases const rect = cameraWrapper.getBoundingClientRect(); const W = Math.round(rect.width * window.devicePixelRatio); const H = Math.round(rect.height * window.devicePixelRatio); compositeCanvas.width = W; compositeCanvas.height = H; compositeCanvas.style.width = rect.width + 'px'; compositeCanvas.style.height = rect.height + 'px'; segCanvas.width = videoEl.videoWidth || 640; segCanvas.height = videoEl.videoHeight || 854; camPrompt.innerHTML = `
✨
AI 模型載入中…
`; // Pre-render background prerenderBg(W, H); // Init segmentation await initSegmentation(); cameraReady = true; camPrompt.style.display = 'none'; shootBtn.disabled = false; startRenderLoop(); } catch(e) { camPrompt.innerHTML = `
⚠️
無法取得相機權限
請允許瀏覽器使用相機
`; console.error(e); } } function prerenderBg(W, H) { const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas'); offscreen.width = W; offscreen.height = H; if (selectedBg) selectedBg.draw(offscreen.getContext('2d'), W, H); bgImageCache.current = offscreen; } function stopAll() { cameraReady = false; segmentationReady = false; if(animFrameId) cancelAnimationFrame(animFrameId); if(selfieSegmentation) { selfieSegmentation.close(); selfieSegmentation = null; } if(stream) { stream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop()); stream = null; } } // ============================================================ // RENDER LOOP // ============================================================ let frameCount = 0; async function startRenderLoop() { if(!cameraReady) return; const ctx = compositeCanvas.getContext('2d'); const W = compositeCanvas.width; const H = compositeCanvas.height; async function loop() { if(!cameraReady) return; // Process every frame for more accurate segmentation if(segmentationReady && selfieSegmentation) { try { await selfieSegmentation.send({ image: videoEl }); } catch(e) {} } frameCount++; // Draw background if(bgImageCache.current) { ctx.drawImage(bgImageCache.current, 0, 0, W, H); } else { ctx.fillStyle = '#111'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H); } if(segmentationReady && lastSegResult && lastSegResult.segmentationMask) { // Use compositeCanvas size throughout for consistency const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas'); tempCanvas.width = W; tempCanvas.height = H; const tCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d'); // Draw video mirrored (only for front camera) - full W x H tCtx.save(); if(facingMode === 'user') { tCtx.translate(W, 0); tCtx.scale(-1, 1); } tCtx.drawImage(videoEl, 0, 0, W, H); tCtx.restore(); // Draw mask with soft edge blur (gentle, preserves body shape) const maskCanvas = document.createElement('canvas'); maskCanvas.width = W; maskCanvas.height = H; const mCtx = maskCanvas.getContext('2d'); // For rear camera: slightly stronger blur to smooth jagged edges const blurAmt = facingMode === 'user' ? '2px' : '3px'; mCtx.filter = 'blur(' + blurAmt + ')'; mCtx.drawImage(lastSegResult.segmentationMask, 0, 0, W, H); mCtx.filter = 'none'; // Temporal smoothing: blend with previous mask frame for stability if(window._prevMask) { mCtx.globalAlpha = 0.35; mCtx.drawImage(window._prevMask, 0, 0, W, H); mCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0; } // Save current mask for next frame window._prevMask = maskCanvas; // Apply mask tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'destination-in'; tCtx.drawImage(maskCanvas, 0, 0, W, H); tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over'; // Subtle color blend with background (makes composite look natural) const bgCtx = bgImageCache.current ? bgImageCache.current.getContext('2d') : null; if(bgCtx) { try { const bgSample = bgCtx.getImageData(Math.round(W*0.3), Math.round(H*0.3), Math.round(W*0.4), Math.round(H*0.4)); let rSum=0, gSum=0, bSum=0, cnt=0; for(let i=0;i10){ pd.data[i] =Math.round(pd.data[i] *(1-blend)+bgR*blend); pd.data[i+1]=Math.round(pd.data[i+1]*(1-blend)+bgG*blend); pd.data[i+2]=Math.round(pd.data[i+2]*(1-blend)+bgB*blend); } } tCtx.putImageData(pd,0,0); } catch(e) {} } // Draw person naturally over background ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas, 0, 0, W, H); } else { // Fallback: draw video full size ctx.save(); if(facingMode === 'user') { ctx.translate(W, 0); ctx.scale(-1, 1); } ctx.drawImage(videoEl, 0, 0, W, H); ctx.restore(); } // Timestamp (live preview - bottom left) (function() { const now = new Date(); const p = n => String(n).padStart(2,'0'); const ts = now.getFullYear() + '-' + p(now.getMonth()+1) + '-' + p(now.getDate()) + ' ' + p(now.getHours()) + ':' + p(now.getMinutes()); const fontSize = Math.round(W * 0.052); ctx.save(); ctx.font = fontSize + "px 'DSEG7 Classic', monospace"; const tw = ctx.measureText(ts).width; const pad = 16; const bx = 14, by = H - fontSize - 28; ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.82)'; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.roundRect(bx - pad/2, by - pad/2, tw + pad, fontSize + pad, 8); ctx.fill(); ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,100,0,0.18)'; ctx.textAlign = 'left'; ctx.textBaseline = 'top'; ctx.fillText(ts, bx, by); ctx.fillStyle = '#FFA500'; ctx.shadowColor = '#FF8C00'; ctx.shadowBlur = 8; ctx.fillText(ts, bx, by); ctx.shadowBlur = 0; ctx.restore(); })(); // Watermark ctx.save(); ctx.font = 'bold ' + Math.round(W*0.032) + "px 'Space Mono', monospace"; ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)'; ctx.textAlign = 'right'; ctx.textBaseline = 'alphabetic'; ctx.fillText('📚 圖書館打卡', W - 14, H - 12); ctx.restore(); animFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(loop); } loop(); } // ============================================================ // SHOOT // ============================================================ shootBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { if(shooting || !cameraReady) return; shooting = true; shootBtn.disabled = true; backBtn.disabled = true; let count = 3; countdown.style.opacity = '1'; countdown.textContent = count; const tick = setInterval(() => { count--; if(count > 0) { countdown.textContent = count; } else { clearInterval(tick); countdown.style.opacity = '0'; capturePhoto(); } }, 900); }); function capturePhoto() { // Flash flashOverlay.style.transition = 'opacity 0.08s'; flashOverlay.style.opacity = '1'; setTimeout(() => { flashOverlay.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s'; flashOverlay.style.opacity = '0'; }, 80); const W = compositeCanvas.width; const H = compositeCanvas.height; finalCanvas.width = W; finalCanvas.height = H; const fctx = finalCanvas.getContext('2d'); // Copy current composite frame fctx.drawImage(compositeCanvas, 0, 0); // Add gold frame fctx.strokeStyle = '#e8a030'; fctx.lineWidth = Math.max(4, W*0.008); const inset = fctx.lineWidth/2; roundRect(fctx, inset, inset, W-inset*2, H-inset*2, 16); fctx.stroke(); // Corners const cs = W*0.07, ci = 18; fctx.strokeStyle = '#e8a030'; fctx.lineWidth = Math.max(3, W*0.006); [[ci,ci,1,1],[W-ci,ci,-1,1],[ci,H-ci,1,-1],[W-ci,H-ci,-1,-1]].forEach(([cx,cy,dx,dy]) => { fctx.beginPath(); fctx.moveTo(cx+dx*cs,cy); fctx.lineTo(cx,cy); fctx.lineTo(cx,cy+dy*cs); fctx.stroke(); }); // Timestamp on final photo (same style as live preview) (function() { const now = new Date(); const p = n => String(n).padStart(2,'0'); const ts = now.getFullYear() + '-' + p(now.getMonth()+1) + '-' + p(now.getDate()) + ' ' + p(now.getHours()) + ':' + p(now.getMinutes()); const fontSize = Math.round(W * 0.052); fctx.save(); fctx.font = fontSize + "px 'DSEG7 Classic', monospace"; const tw2 = fctx.measureText(ts).width; const pad = 16; const bx2 = 14, by2 = H - fontSize - 28; fctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.82)'; fctx.beginPath(); fctx.roundRect(bx2 - pad/2, by2 - pad/2, tw2 + pad, fontSize + pad, 8); fctx.fill(); fctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,100,0,0.18)'; fctx.textAlign = 'left'; fctx.textBaseline = 'top'; fctx.fillText(ts, bx2, by2); fctx.fillStyle = '#FFA500'; fctx.shadowColor = '#FF8C00'; fctx.shadowBlur = 8; fctx.fillText(ts, bx2, by2); fctx.shadowBlur = 0; fctx.restore(); })(); // Badge (bottom right) const fs = Math.round(W*0.036); fctx.font = 'bold ' + fs + "px 'Space Mono', monospace"; const text = '📚 圖書館打卡'; const tw = fctx.measureText(text).width + 22; const bx = W - tw - 10, by = H - fs - 18; fctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(26,18,9,0.65)'; roundRect(fctx, bx, by, tw, fs+12, 8); fctx.fill(); fctx.fillStyle = '#e8a030'; fctx.textAlign = 'center'; fctx.textBaseline = 'alphabetic'; fctx.fillText(text, bx+tw/2, by+fs+2); stopAll(); showScreen(3); shooting = false; shootBtn.disabled = false; backBtn.disabled = false; } function roundRect(ctx, x, y, w, h, r) { ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x+r,y); ctx.lineTo(x+w-r,y); ctx.arcTo(x+w,y,x+w,y+r,r); ctx.lineTo(x+w,y+h-r); ctx.arcTo(x+w,y+h,x+w-r,y+h,r); ctx.lineTo(x+r,y+h); ctx.arcTo(x,y+h,x,y+h-r,r); ctx.lineTo(x,y+r); ctx.arcTo(x,y,x+r,y,r); ctx.closePath(); } // Save button → fullscreen display const fullscreenOverlay = document.getElementById('fullscreenOverlay'); const fullscreenImg = document.getElementById('fullscreenImg'); const fullscreenClose = document.getElementById('fullscreenClose'); document.getElementById('downloadBtn').addEventListener('click', () => { // Show image fullscreen for easy long-press save fullscreenImg.src = finalCanvas.toDataURL('image/png'); fullscreenOverlay.classList.add('show'); }); fullscreenClose.addEventListener('click', () => { fullscreenOverlay.classList.remove('show'); }); function showToast(msg) { toast.textContent = msg; toast.classList.add('show'); setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove('show'), 2500); } window.addEventListener('resize', () => { if(cameraReady) { const rect = cameraWrapper.getBoundingClientRect(); const W = Math.round(rect.width * window.devicePixelRatio); const H = Math.round(rect.height * window.devicePixelRatio); compositeCanvas.width = W; compositeCanvas.height = H; compositeCanvas.style.width = rect.width+'px'; compositeCanvas.style.height = rect.height+'px'; prerenderBg(W, H); } });
